      <p>This is a list of countries by order of appearance in the <a href="/wiki/Fragile_States_Index" title="Fragile States Index">Fragile States Index</a> (formerly the Failed States Index) of the United States <a href="/wiki/Think_tank" title="Think tank">think tank</a> <a href="/wiki/Fund_for_Peace" title="Fund for Peace">Fund for Peace</a>. </p>
      <p>A fragile <a href="/wiki/Sovereign_state" title="Sovereign state">state</a> has several attributes. Common indicators include a state whose <a href="/wiki/Central_government" title="Central government">central government</a> is so weak or ineffective that it has little practical control over much of its territory; non-provision of <a href="/wiki/Public_services" class="mw-redirect" title="Public services">public services</a>; widespread corruption and criminality; refugees and involuntary movement of populations; and sharp economic decline.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup> Since 2005, the index has been published annually by the Fund for Peace and the magazine <i><a href="/wiki/Foreign_Policy" title="Foreign Policy">Foreign Policy</a></i>. The list has been cited by journalists and academics in making broad comparative points about countries or regions.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup> </p>
      <p>This is the list for 2020,<sup id="cite_ref-FSI_2020_4-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FSI_2020-4">[4]</a></sup> with comparisons of each country's current score to previous years' indices. </p>
      <p>The report uses 12 factors to determine the rating for each nation, including security threats, economic implosion, <a href="/wiki/Human_rights" title="Human rights">human rights</a> violations and refugee flows. </p>

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Indicators_of_a_fragile_state">Indicators of a fragile state</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_countries_by_Fragile_States_Index&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Indicators of a fragile state">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <p>The following factors are used by <a href="/wiki/Fund_For_Peace" class="mw-redirect" title="Fund For Peace">Fund For Peace</a> to ascertain the status of a country.<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">[5]</a></sup> </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Social">Social</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_countries_by_Fragile_States_Index&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Social">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <ul>
       <li>Mounting demographic pressures and tribal, ethnic and/or religious conflicts.</li> 
       <li>Massive internal and external displacement of refugees, creating severe <a href="/wiki/Humanitarian_crisis" title="Humanitarian crisis">humanitarian emergencies</a>.</li> 
       <li>Widespread vengeance-seeking group grievances.</li> 
       <li>Chronic and sustained <a href="/wiki/Emigration" title="Emigration">human flight</a>.</li>
      </ul> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Economic">Economic</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_countries_by_Fragile_States_Index&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Economic">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <ul>
       <li>Widespread <a href="/wiki/Corruption" title="Corruption">corruption</a></li> 
       <li>High <a href="/wiki/Economic_inequality" title="Economic inequality">economic inequality</a></li> 
       <li>Uneven economic development along group lines.</li> 
       <li>Severe economic decline.</li>
      </ul> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Political">Political</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_countries_by_Fragile_States_Index&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Political">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <ul>
       <li>Delegitimization of the state.</li> 
       <li>Deterioration of public services.</li> 
       <li>Suspension or arbitrary application of law; widespread <a href="/wiki/Human_rights#Human_rights_violations" title="Human rights">human rights abuses</a>.</li> 
       <li><a href="/wiki/Security_forces" title="Security forces">Security forces</a> operating as a "<a href="/wiki/State_within_a_state" class="mw-redirect" title="State within a state">state within a state</a>" often with impunity.</li> 
       <li>Rise of factionalized elites.</li> 
       <li>Intervention of external political agents and foreign states.</li>
      </ul> 
      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Fragile_States_Index_2020">Fragile States Index 2020</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_countries_by_Fragile_States_Index&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Fragile States Index 2020">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
